    @staticmethod
    def merge_sort(arr):
        """ Merge Sort
            Complexity: O(n log(n))
        """
        size = len(arr)
        half = size/2
        # Our recursive base case
        if size <= 1:
            return arr
        # Perform merge_sort recursively on both halves

    @staticmethod
    def merge(left, right):
        """ Merge helper
            Complexity: O(n)
